<rate>1< /rate>< text>
The food is not very good but the boba and smoothies are decent. The popcorn chicken (despite being made fresh) was rubbery and soft, if I didn't know any better I would compare the texture to that of raw chicken. I'm sure it has something to do with it being dark meat, but it was also slimy inside? Not really sure how else to describe it, perhaps due to the texture of the meat and grease from the oil. All in all not pleasant. The egg rolls were not vegetarian and the sweet and sour sauce had chili and garlic (I'm allergic to garlic) so that was a waste also. If you are looking for a quick local boba, this is fine. If you are hungry do yourself a favor and go somewhere else.

11/22- Update, this place just lost the few stars it previously had because I drove all the way from roseville and they decided to be closed 20mins early and turned away myself and two other groups of people. I'll take my business to The Bomb in roseville then!< /text>

I originally wanted to take my mom over to somi somi yesterday but it was packed like crazy. Luckily, I was able to find this shop! < Text>
This is a cute little dessert place for those who tend to have a sweet tooth.
I met the owner shortly after they had their soft opening and she was very friendly and caring. It was evident that she prioritized quality over quantity (i.e. the drinks are always made from fresh ingredients). The menu items are also reasonably priced, especially for those who are ballin on a budget... (#me)
This place also has a decent amount of space to play games, study, hang out, or read.
I've been here a few times and the atmosphere is always very relaxed.
Overall, it's worth a try!</Text>

Just found this the other day on the way home from donating plasma. It's just a few blocks from my house and I noticed they had a drive thru and I had to pick up something for my picky 15 year olds daughter, for dinner,  on the way home. So I got the usual bean and cheese burrito for her. Oddly enough she loved it. She likes about 30% of bean and cheese burritos that are purchased for her btw. Food was substandard. Fajitas are supposed to be strips of beef or chicken grilled over an open fire and seasoned served with seared bell peppers. What I got was diced up carne asada burrito meat, decidedly not cooked over an open fire. mixed with nearly raw bell pepper chunks. I also ordered a side of guacamole. What I got was barely guacamole. It was virtually runny and tasteless. Very unimaginative. Taco Bell has better guacamole. < Text>
Pleasant space with friendly bartenders.  I only have two real complaints, both relating to the fact that it's very hard to socialize with friends.   1. The seating inside is at at least 4 different heights....super low sofas, high stools, low stools, medium chairs... all different.  You wind up talking to someone's belly button, or they into your knees.   2. The audio from the pianists (which are quite good, btw) tends to be over amplified - usually  much louder in the front of the bar than right at the piano.   I would suggest more present at the piano where people want to listen 100%  and more background in the front and outside where folks want to be more social.  All that said, it's nice to have a real piano bar back in the neighborhood.< /Text>

< text>
If you have a pet that eats live food, particularly feeder fish, this is by far the best place in Elk Grove to get them. The tanks are well maintained and always full of a unique collection of species. The staff in the Aquatic department is knowledgeable and helpful to a T. They always offer quality insight without coming off as sanctimonious, a fine line to walk. You can tell the staff at Pet Club are all pet owners and are actively interested in animal welfare and well being.< /text>
